<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Item
4.01. Changes in Registrant&#8217;s Certifying Accountant.</b></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><i>(a)
Departure of Independent Registered Public Accounting Firm</i></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">On
December 9, 2025, upon the recommendation</span> <span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">of
the Audit Committee of the Board of Directors (the &#8220;Audit Committee&#8221;) of FG Nexus Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) and upon
the approval of the Board of Directors of the Company (the &#8220;Board&#8221;), the Company accepted the resignation of Haskell &amp;
White LLP (&#8220;H&amp;W&#8221;) as the Company&#8217;s independent registered public accounting firm, effective immediately.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">H&amp;W
audited the consolidated financial statements of the Company for each of the fiscal years ended December 31, 2024 and 2023 (collectively
referred to as the &#8220;financial statements&#8221;). The reports of H&amp;W on such consolidated financial statements did not contain
an adverse opinion or disclaimer of opinion and was not qualified or modified as to&#160;uncertainty, audit scope or accounting principles.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">During
the two most recent fiscal years ended December 31, 2024 and 2023, and the subsequent interim periods through the date of resignation,
there were (i) no disagreements (as that term is defined in Item&#160;304(a)(1)(iv)&#160;of&#160;Regulation S-K&#160;and the related
instructions) with H&amp;W on any matter of accounting principles or practices, financial statement disclosure, or auditing scope or
procedure, which disagreement, if not resolved to the satisfaction of H&amp;W, would have caused them to make reference thereto in their
report on the consolidated financial statements and (ii) no &#8220;reportable events&#8221; (as that term is defined in Item&#160;304(a)(1)(v)&#160;of&#160;Regulation
S-K).</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">The
Company has provided H&amp;W a copy of the above disclosure made in this Current Report on Form 8-K and has requested that
H&amp;W provide a letter addressed to the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission stating whether H&amp;W agrees with the statements
made by the Company in response to this Item 4.01 and, if not, stating the respects in which it does not agree. A copy of H&amp;W&#8217;s
letter is attached as Exhibit 16.1 to this Current Report on Form&#160;8-K.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><i>(b)
Engagement of New Independent Registered Public Accounting Firm</i></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">On
December 10, 2025, upon the recommendation of the Audit Committee and upon the approval of the Board, the Company engaged BPM LLP (&#8220;BPM&#8221;)
as the Company&#8217;s independent registered public accounting firm to audit the Company&#8217;s consolidated financial statements for
the fiscal year ending December 31, 2025, effective on December 10, 2025.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 47.05pt"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">During
the fiscal years ended December 31, 2024 and 2023, and the subsequent interim period through the date of BPM&#8217;s engagement, neither
the Company nor anyone acting on its behalf consulted BPM regarding either (i) the application of accounting principles to a specified
transaction, either completed or proposed, or the type of audit opinion that might be rendered on the Company&#8217;s consolidated financial
statements and neither a written report nor oral advice was provided to the Company by BPM that BPM concluded was an important factor
considered by the Company in reaching a decision as to such accounting, auditing, or financial reporting issue; or (ii) any matter that
was either the subject of a &#8220;disagreement&#8221; (as that term is defined in Item&#160;304(a)(1)(iv)&#160;of&#160;Regulation S-K&#160;and
the related instructions) or a &#8220;reportable event&#8221; (as that term is defined in Item&#160;304(a)(1)(v)&#160;of&#160;Regulation
S-K).</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 47.05pt"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

  <tr style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top">
